Suite can open a wide variety of file formats.\r\n\r\n- Opening text documents\r\nIn addition to OpenDocument formats (.odt, .ott, .oth, .odm, .sxw, .stw, and .sxg ), Word Editor can open the following text document formats:\r\n• Microsoft Word 2007 - 2019 (.docx)\r\n• Microsoft Word 6.0/95/97/2000/XP (.doc and .dot)\r\n• Microsoft Word 2003 XML (.xml)\r\n• Microsoft Word 2007 XML (.docx, (.xml)\r\n• Unified Office Format text (.uot, .uof)\r\n• Ichitaro 8/9/10/11 (.jtd and .jtt)\r\n• Hangul WP 97 (.hwp)\r\n• T602 Document (.602, .txt)\r\n• AportisDoc (Palm) (.pdb)\r\n• Pocket Word (.psw)\r\nWhen opening .htm or .html files (used for web pages), Ultra Office Suite customizes Writer for working with these files.\r\n\r\n- Opening spreadsheets\r\nIn addition to OpenDocument formats (.ods, .ots, .sxc and .stc), Excel Editor can open the following spreadsheet formats:\r\n• Microsoft Excel 2007 - 2019 (.xlsx)\r\n• Microsoft Excel 97/2000/XP (.xls, .xlw, and .xlt)\r\n• Microsoft Excel 4.x–5.0/95 (.xls, .xlw, and .xlt)\r\n• Microsoft Excel 2003 XML (.xml)\r\n• Microsoft Excel 2007 XML (.xlsx, .xlsm, .xltx, .xltm)\r\n• Microsoft Excel 2007 binary (.xlsb)\r\n• Lotus 1-2-3 (.wk1, .wks, and .123)\r\n• Data Interchange Format (.dif)\r\n• Rich Text Format (.rtf)\r\n• Text CSV (.csv and .txt)\r\n• StarCalc formats (.sdc and .vor)\r\n• dBASE (.dbf)\r\n• SYLK (.slk)\r\n• Unified Office Format spreadsheet (.uos, .uof)\r\n• .htm and .html files, including Web page queries\r\n• Pocket Excel (pxl)\r\n• Quattro Pro 6.0 (.wb2)\r\n\r\n- Opening presentations\r\nIn addition to OpenDocument formats (.odp, .odg, .otp,.sxi, and .sti), PowerPoint Editor can open the following presentation formats:\r\n• Microsoft PowerPoint 2007 - 2019 (.pptx)\r\n• Microsoft PowerPoint .uof)\r\n• CGM – Computer Graphics Metafile (.cgm)\r\n\r\n- Opening graphic files\r\nIn addition to OpenDocument formats (.odg, .otg, .sxd,.std,.sxd, .std), Draw can open the following graphic files\r\nIn addition to OpenDocument Formula (.odf) files, Math can open the format (.sxm), StarMath, (.smf), and MathML (.mml) files.\r\nWhen opening a Word document that contains an embedded equation editor object, if the option for it is checked in Tools > Options > Load/Save > Microsoft Office, the object will be automatically converted to an Ultra Office Suite Math object.\r\n\r\n***File formats Ultra Office Suite can save to\r\n\r\n-Saving text documents\r\nIn addition to OpenDocument formats (.odt and .ott), Word Editor can save in these formats:\r\n•
